            $.extend($.fn.dataTable.defaults, {

            $.extend($.fn.dataTableExt.oSort, {
                "smart-asc": function (a, b) {
                    if (a === b)
                        return 0;

                    if (a === "&nbsp;")
                        return 1;
                    else if (b === "&nbsp;")
                        return -1;

                    if (a.length === 8 && a.charAt(2) === ":" && a.charAt(5) === ":" &&
                        b.length === 8 && b.charAt(2) === ":" && b.charAt(5) === ":")
                    {
                        // Timespan format
                        parseA = 
(parseInt(a.substring(0, 2)) * 3600) + (parseInt(a.substring(3, 5)) * 
60) + parseInt(a.substring(6, 8));
                        parseB = 
(parseInt(b.substring(0, 2)) * 3600) + (parseInt(b.substring(3, 5)) * 
60) + parseInt(b.substring(6, 8));
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        // Check for Percent format, and handle international formatting
                        var parseA = parseFloat(a.replace(",", "").replace(".", "."));
                        var parseB = parseFloat(b.replace(",", "").replace(".", "."));

                        if (isNaN(parseA))
                        {
                            // Text format
                            parseA = a;

                            // Remove HTML so we are only sorting on visible text
                            var parseHTMLA = $.parseHTML(parseA);
                            if (typeof parseHTMLA !== "undefined" && parseHTMLA.length === 1)
                                parseA = parseHTMLA[0].textContent.split('\n')[0];

                            parseA = parseA.toLowerCase();

                            // Check for Percent format once more
                            var parseAInner = parseFloat(parseA.replace(",", "").replace(".", "."));
                            if (!isNaN(parseAInner))
                                parseA = parseAInner;
                        }

                        if (isNaN(parseB))
                        {
                            // Text format
                            parseB = b;

                            // Remove HTML so we are only sorting on visible text
                            var parseHTMLB = $.parseHTML(parseB);
                            if (typeof parseHTMLB !== "undefined" && parseHTMLB.length === 1)
                                parseB = parseHTMLB[0].textContent.split('\n')[0];

                            parseB = parseB.toLowerCase();

                            // Check for Percent format once more
                            var parseBInner = parseFloat(parseB.replace(",", "").replace(".", "."));
                            if (!isNaN(parseBInner))
                                parseB = parseBInner;
                        }
                    }

                    if (parseA > parseB)
                        return 1;
                    else
                        return -1;
                },

                "smart-desc": function (a, b) {
                    if (a === b)
                        return 0;

                    if (a === "&nbsp;")
                        return 1;
                    else if (b === "&nbsp;")
                        return -1;

                    if (a.length === 8 && a.charAt(2) === ":" && a.charAt(5) === ":" &&
                        b.length === 8 && b.charAt(2) === ":" && b.charAt(5) === ":")
                    {
                        // Timespan format
                        parseA = 
(parseInt(a.substring(0, 2)) * 3600) + (parseInt(a.substring(3, 5)) * 
60) + parseInt(a.substring(6, 8));
                        parseB = 
(parseInt(b.substring(0, 2)) * 3600) + (parseInt(b.substring(3, 5)) * 
60) + parseInt(b.substring(6, 8));
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        // Check for Percent format, and handle international formatting
                        var parseA = parseFloat(a.replace(",", "").replace(".", "."));
                        var parseB = parseFloat(b.replace(",", "").replace(".", "."));

                        if (isNaN(parseA))
                        {
                            // Text format
                            parseA = a;

                            // Remove HTML so we are only sorting on visible text
                            var parseHTMLA = $.parseHTML(parseA);
                            if (typeof parseHTMLA !== "undefined" && parseHTMLA.length === 1)
                                parseA = parseHTMLA[0].textContent.split('\n')[0];

                            parseA = parseA.toLowerCase();

                            // Check for Percent format once more
                            var parseAInner = parseFloat(parseA.replace(",", "").replace(".", "."));
                            if (!isNaN(parseAInner))
                                parseA = parseAInner;
                        }

                        if (isNaN(parseB))
                        {
                            // Text format
                            parseB = b;

                            // Remove HTML so we are only sorting on visible text
                            var parseHTMLB = $.parseHTML(parseB);
                            if (typeof parseHTMLB !== "undefined" && parseHTMLB.length === 1)
                                parseB = parseHTMLB[0].textContent.split('\n')[0];

                            parseB = parseB.toLowerCase();

                            // Check for Percent format once more
                            var parseBInner = parseFloat(parseB.replace(",", "").replace(".", "."));
                            if (!isNaN(parseBInner))
                                parseB = parseBInner;
                        }
                    }

                    if (parseB > parseA)
                        return 1;
                    else
                        return -1;
                }
            });

            $(document).ready(function ()
            {
                // Function to Style RadGrid Stripes On DataTable Events
                RadGridReorderStripes = function (RadGrid) {
                    $("tr", RadGrid).removeClass("rgRow rgAltRow");
                    $("tr.odd", RadGrid).addClass("rgRow");
                    $("tr.even", RadGrid).addClass("rgAltRow");
                };

                // All DataTable Draw Events Should Restripe
                $(document).on("draw.dt", 
"table", function () { if ($(this).hasClass("dataTable")) 
RadGridReorderStripes(this); })

                // Set up Back to Top Link
                $("#back-top").hide();
                $(window).scroll(function (e) {
 if ($(this).scrollTop() > 100) { $('#back-top').fadeIn(); } else { 
$('#back-top').fadeOut(); } });
                $('#back-top a').click(function (e) { $('body,html').animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, 500); return false; });

                // Set Up Sign Out Menu Icon
                $("#LoginStatus").html("<i class='fa fa-sign-out'></i>");

                // Keep Focus on Player Search Menu Popup
                $(".dropdown-menu input").click(function (e) { e.stopPropagation(); });

                // Focus on Player Name Textbox when Clicking on Player Search
                
$(".playerSearchDropdown").click(function (e) { setTimeout(function () {
 $(".TextBoxPlayerSearch").focus(); }, 10); });

                function PlayerSearchRedirect()
                {
                    window.location.href = "/PlayerSearch?Name=" + $(".TextBoxPlayerSearch").val();
                }

                $("#ButtonPlayerSearch").click(function (e) { PlayerSearchRedirect(); });

                $(".TextBoxPlayerSearch").keydown(function (e) {
                    if (e.keyCode === 13 /* Enter key */)
                    {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        PlayerSearchRedirect();
                    }
                });

                // Use mouseover popups for tooltips
                $(document).on("mouseenter", 
"tr[title], img[title], div[title], tr[data-tooltip], img[data-tooltip],
 div[data-tooltip]", function() {
					var title = getTitle(this);
					if (title) {
						addTooltip(this, title);
					}
            	})

            	$(document).on("mouseleave", 
"tr[title], img[title], div[title], tr[data-tooltip], img[data-tooltip],
 div[data-tooltip]", function() {
            		$(this).siblings('span').remove();
            	})

                // Adjust Datatables Fixed Header, toggling visibility if the user is switching tabs
                $(document).on("click", "body", function (e) {
                    setTimeout(function(){ 
$(".dataTable").not(".RadGridReplayCharacterScoreResults 
.dataTable").DataTable().fixedHeader.adjust(); }, 0);
                });

                $(document).on("init.dt", "body", function (e, settings, json) {
                    $("div.dt-buttons").each(function() {
                        $(this).insertAfter($(this).parent().find("input[type='search']"));
                    });
                });
            });

            var getTitle = function(element) {
            	if (element.title) {
            		element.setAttribute("data-tooltip", element.title);
            		element.removeAttribute("title");
            	}
            	return element.getAttribute("data-tooltip");
            };

            var addTooltip = function(target, text) {
            	$("> span", target).remove();
            	var span = document.createElement("span");
            	span.className = "titlePopup";
            	span.innerHTML = text.replace(/^([^:]+):/, "<b>$1</b>");
            	$(target).after(span);
            };

                    setRefreshAd(slots, refreshRate, refreshLimit) {
                        if (slots && slots.length > 0) {                            
                            var refreshCount = 1;
                            var refreshInterval = null;
                            refreshInterval = setInterval(function () {
                                if (refreshCount++ >= refreshLimit) {
                                    // We've hit the refresh limit, stop the refresh
                                    clearInterval(refreshInterval);
                                    return;
                                }					
                                googletag.pubads().refresh(slots);
                            }, refreshRate * 1000);
                        }
                    },
                    setTO(id) {
                        var self = this;
                        setTimeout(function () {
                            if (document.getElementById(id) != null) {
                                googletag.cmd.push(function () { googletag.display(id); });
                            }
                            else {
                                self.setTO(id);
                            }
                        }, 300);
                    },
                    parse: function (config) {
                        if (typeof googletag !== "undefined") {
                            var self = this;
                            googletag.cmd.push(function () {
                                var ids = self.addSlots(config);

                                googletag.pubads().enableAsyncRendering();

                                googletag.enableServices();
                                var slots = [];
                                for (var i in ids) {
                                    if (ids[i]) {
                                        self.setTO(ids[i][0]);
                                        slots.push(ids[i][1]);
                                    }
                                }
                                self.setRefreshAd(slots, config.refreshRate, config.refreshLimit);
                            });
                        }
                    }

                /**
                 * Helper for managing sessionStorage.
                 *
                 * @type {sessionStorage}
                 */
                $WH.sessionStorage = {
                    /**
                     * Test if sessionStorage is supported and usable.
                     *
                     * @returns boolean
                     **/
                    isSupported: function () {
                        var supported;
                        try {
                            supported = 'sessionStorage' in window && window['sessionStorage'] !== null;
                        } catch (e) {
                            supported = false;
                        }

                        if (supported) {
                            try {
                                sessionStorage.setItem('test', '123');
                                supported = sessionStorage.getItem('test') == '123';
                                sessionStorage.removeItem('test');
                            } catch (e) {
                                supported = false;
                            }
                        }

                        $WH.sessionStorage.isSupported = (function (supported) {
                            return supported;
                        }).bind(null, supported);
                        return supported;
                    },

                    /**
                     * Sets a session storage variable
                     *
                     * @params key
                     * @params value
                     */
                    set: function (key, value) {
                        if (!$WH.sessionStorage.isSupported()) {
                            return;
                        }

                        sessionStorage.setItem(key, value);
                    },
                    /**
                     * Gets a session storage variable
                     *
                     * @params key
                     * @returns *
                     */
                    get: function (key) {
                        if (!$WH.sessionStorage.isSupported()) {
                            return;
                        }

                        return sessionStorage.getItem(key);
                    },
                    /**
                     * Deletes a session storage variable
                     *
                     * @params key
                     */
                    remove: function (key) {
                        if (!$WH.sessionStorage.isSupported()) {
                            return;
                        }

                        sessionStorage.removeItem(key);
                    }
                };

                var CONFIG_PARSER = {};
                var ad_config = {};

                CONFIG_PARSER.setEvent = function (ab) {
                    if (!ga) {

                        document.cookie = "ab-value=" + ab + "; domain=" + window.location.host + "; path=/";
                    }
                };

                CONFIG_PARSER.getInclusion = function (config) {
                    if (typeof (I11C) !== "undefined" && I11C.Morph == 1) {
                        return "_Instart";
                    } else {
                        return "";
                    }
                };

                function getParameterByName(name, url) {
                    if (!url) url = window.location.href;
                    name = name.replace(/[\[\]]/g, "\\$&");
                    var regex = new RegExp("[?&]" + name + "(=([^&#]*)|&|#|$)"),
                        results = regex.exec(url);
                    if (!results) return null;
                    if (!results[2]) return '';
                    return decodeURIComponent(results[2].replace(/\+/g, " "));
                }

                CONFIG_PARSER.getSiteAB = function () {
                    if (!AD_CONFIG.active) {
                        CONFIG_PARSER.setEvent('A');
                        return configA;
                    }
                    var sessionKey = 'adAB-' + AD_CONFIG.id;

                    var override = getParameterByName('ab_override');
                    var ab = $WH.sessionStorage.get(sessionKey);
                    if (AD_CONFIG.abTestOptions.indexOf(ab) < 0) {
                        if (Math.random() < AD_CONFIG.bPercent * .01) {
                            ab = 'B';
                        } else {
                            ab = 'A';
                        }
                        $WH.sessionStorage.set(sessionKey, ab);
                    }
                    if (override && AD_CONFIG.abTestOptions.indexOf(override) > -1) {
                        ab = override;
                        $WH.sessionStorage.set(sessionKey, ab);
                    }
                    CONFIG_PARSER.setEvent(ab);
                    if (ab == 'A') return configA;
                    if (ab == 'B') return configB;
                }

                CONFIG_PARSER.GO = function () {
                    ad_config = CONFIG_PARSER.getSiteAB();
                    google_parser.parse(ad_config);
                };

                CONFIG_PARSER.GO();
                		

                
                var advertisementOffsetTop = 80;
                var advertisementOffsetTopAnimate = advertisementOffsetTop - 40;
                if (advertisementOffsetTopAnimate < 0)
                    advertisementOffsetTopAnimate = 0;
                var isVerticalAdvertisementFixed = false;
                function FixVerticalAdvertisement(forceRefresh)
                {
                    if (forceRefresh)
                        isVerticalAdvertisementFixed = !isVerticalAdvertisementFixed;

                    var scrollTop = $(document).scrollTop();
                    var advertisementPlaceholder = $("#advertisementPlaceholder");
                    var advertisementTop = advertisementPlaceholder.offset().top;
                    var advertisementLeft = advertisementPlaceholder.width() + advertisementPlaceholder.position().left;

                    var verticalAdvertisements = $("#mb_adslot_1, #mb_adslot_2");
                    if (!isVerticalAdvertisementFixed && advertisementTop - scrollTop < advertisementOffsetTop)
                    {
                        isVerticalAdvertisementFixed = true;
                        verticalAdvertisements.css("position", "fixed");
                        verticalAdvertisements.css("top", advertisementOffsetTopAnimate + "px");
                        verticalAdvertisements.css("left", (advertisementLeft + 30) + "px");

                        if (!forceRefresh)
                        {
                            
                            verticalAdvertisements.css("top", advertisementOffsetTopAnimate + "px");
                            verticalAdvertisements.animate({ top: advertisementOffsetTop + "px" });
                        }
                        else
                            
                            verticalAdvertisements.css("top", advertisementOffsetTop + "px");
                    }
                    else if 
(isVerticalAdvertisementFixed && advertisementTop - scrollTop 
>= advertisementOffsetTop) {
                        isVerticalAdvertisementFixed = false;
                        verticalAdvertisements.css("position", "absolute");
                        verticalAdvertisements.css("top", advertisementTop + "px");
                        verticalAdvertisements.css("left", (advertisementLeft + 30) + "px");
                    }
                }

                var lastHeight = 0;
                $(document).ready(function () {

                    if ($(window).height() >= 600)
                    {
                        FixVerticalAdvertisement();

                        
                        lastHeight = $("iframe.MonkeyBroker-Size41").css("height");
                        function CheckForTopSkin()
                        {
                            var newHeight = $("iframe.MonkeyBroker-Size41").css("height");

                            if (newHeight !== lastHeight)
                            {
                                lastHeight = newHeight;
                                FixVerticalAdvertisement(false);
                            }

                            setTimeout(CheckForTopSkin, 100);
                        }
                        CheckForTopSkin();

                        $(window).scroll(function () {
                            FixVerticalAdvertisement();
                        });

                        $(window).resize(function () {
                            FixVerticalAdvertisement(true);
                        });
                    }
                        
                });

    <script type="text/javascript">

        $(document).ready(function () {

            SetUpDataTables(null, null);

            $("#HeroStatisticsTab").click(function (e) {
                setTimeout(function () { 
$find("ctl00_MainContent_RadHtmlChartSitewideCharacterWinRateByDateTime").repaint();
 }, 10);
            });

            $("#WinRateByGameTimeTab").click(function (e) {
                setTimeout(function () { 
$find("ctl00_MainContent_RadHtmlChartSitewideCharacterWinRateByGameTime").repaint();
 }, 10);
            });

            $("#WinRateByHeroLevelTab").click(function (e) {
                setTimeout(function () { 
$find("ctl00_MainContent_RadHtmlChartSitewideCharacterWinRateByHeroLevel").repaint();
 }, 10);
            });

            $("#WinRateByTalentUpgrade").click(function (e) {
                setTimeout(function () { $find("ctl00_MainContent_RadHtmlChartWinRateByTalentUpgrade").repaint(); }, 10);
            });

        });

        function SetUpDataTables(sender, e)
        {
            if (e !== null && e.get_eventTarget().indexOf("RadDropDownListTalentUpgradeType") !== -1)
                return;

            if ((e === null || (e.get_eventTarget().indexOf("ComboBoxMapName") === -1
                && e.get_eventTarget().indexOf("ComboBoxReplayDateTime") === -1
                && e.get_eventTarget().indexOf("RadGridHeroTalentStatistics") === -1
                && e.get_eventTarget().indexOf("RadDropDownListPopularTalentBuildDisplayMode") === -1)))
            {
                if ($('#RadGridSitewideCharacterWinPercentVsOtherCharacters table .rgNoRecords').length === 0)
                    $('#RadGridSitewideCharacterWinPercentVsOtherCharacters table').DataTable({ "order": [[3, "desc"]] });

                if ($('#RadGridSitewideCharacterWinPercentWithOtherCharacters table .rgNoRecords').length === 0)
                    $('#RadGridSitewideCharacterWinPercentWithOtherCharacters table').DataTable({ "order": [[3, "desc"]] });

                $('#RadGridMapStatistics table').DataTable({ "order": [[3, "desc"]] });
            }

            if ($(".RadGridPopularTalentBuilds table .rgNoRecords").length === 0)
                $(".RadGridPopularTalentBuilds table").DataTable({ "order": [[1, "desc"]] });

            $(".slickTalentBuildCards").slick({
                dots: true,
                variableWidth: true,
                centerMode: true,
                infinite: false
            });

            if ($(".RadHtmlChartWinRateByTalentUpgradeDisabled").length === 0)
                $("#liWinRateByTalentUpgrade").show();
            else
                $("#liWinRateByTalentUpgrade").hide();
        }

        var oldComboBoxLeagueValue = "[]";
        var oldComboBoxMapNameValue = "[]";
        var oldComboBoxReplayDateTimeValue = "[]";

        function OnClientDropDownClosedHandler(sender, eventArgs) {
            var newComboBoxLeagueValue = JSON.stringify($find("ctl00_MainContent_ComboBoxLeague").get_checkedIndices());
            var newComboBoxMapNameValue = JSON.stringify($find("ctl00_MainContent_ComboBoxMapName").get_checkedIndices());
            var 
newComboBoxReplayDateTimeValue = 
JSON.stringify($find("ctl00_MainContent_ComboBoxReplayDateTime").get_checkedIndices());

            if (newComboBoxLeagueValue !== oldComboBoxLeagueValue) {
                oldComboBoxLeagueValue = newComboBoxLeagueValue;
                $find("ctl00_MainContent_RadAjaxManager1").ajaxRequestWithTarget("ctl00$MainContent$ComboBoxLeague", "");
            }
            else if (oldComboBoxMapNameValue !== newComboBoxMapNameValue) {
                oldComboBoxMapNameValue = newComboBoxMapNameValue;
                $find("ctl00_MainContent_RadAjaxManager1").ajaxRequestWithTarget("ctl00$MainContent$ComboBoxMapName", "");
            }
            else if (oldComboBoxReplayDateTimeValue !== newComboBoxReplayDateTimeValue) {
                oldComboBoxReplayDateTimeValue = newComboBoxReplayDateTimeValue;
                
$find("ctl00_MainContent_RadAjaxManager1").ajaxRequestWithTarget("ctl00$MainContent$ComboBoxReplayDateTime",
 "");
            }
        }

        function OnClientSelectedIndexChanged(sender, eventArgs) {
            window.history.replaceState({}, "", "HeroDetails?Hero=" + sender.get_selectedItem().get_value());

            $(".title .section-title").text("英雄细节: " + sender.get_selectedItem().get_text());
        }

    </script>
